\doxysubsection{Member Enumeration Documentation}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classWt_ab8f772c69bc8180c31f9e4f4593b143f}\label{classWt_ab8f772c69bc8180c31f9e4f4593b143f}} 
\index{Wt@{Wt}!AlignmentFlag@{AlignmentFlag}}
\index{AlignmentFlag@{AlignmentFlag}!Wt@{Wt}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{AlignmentFlag}{AlignmentFlag}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum Wt\+::\+Alignment\+Flag\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [strong]}}



Enumeration that specifies a horizontal or a vertical alignment. 

The vertical alignment flags are Alignment\+Flag\+::\+Baseline, Alignment\+Flag\+::\+Sub, Alignment\+Flag\+::\+Super, Alignment\+Flag\+::\+Top, Alignment\+Flag\+::\+Text\+Top, Alignment\+Flag\+::\+Middle, Alignment\+Flag\+::\+Bottom and Alignment\+Flag\+::\+Text\+Bottom.

The horizontal alignment flags are Alignment\+Flag\+::\+Left, Alignment\+Flag\+::\+Right, Alignment\+Flag\+::\+Center and Alignment\+Flag\+::\+Justify.

When used with set\+Vertical\+Alignment(), this applies only to inline widgets and determines how to position itself on the current line, with respect to sibling inline widgets.

When used with \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WContainerWidget_aba13c9e62c74bcba53519ee9cf41f40a}{W\+Table\+Cell\+::set\+Content\+Alignment()}}, this determines the vertical alignment of contents within the table cell.

When used with \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WPainter_afc7fee7dc4d839f78c1c99244da4f486}{W\+Painter\+::draw\+Text()}}, this determines the horizontal and vertical alignment of the text with respect to the bounding rectangle.

When used with \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WContainerWidget_aba13c9e62c74bcba53519ee9cf41f40a}{W\+Container\+Widget\+::set\+Content\+Alignment()}}, this specifies how contents should be aligned horizontally within the container.

Not all values are applicable in all situations. The most commonly used values are Alignment\+Flag\+::\+Left, Alignment\+Flag\+::\+Center, Alignment\+Flag\+::\+Right, Alignment\+Flag\+::\+Bottom, Alignment\+Flag\+::\+Middle and Alignment\+Flag\+::\+Top. \begin{DoxyEnumFields}{Enumerator}

An enumeration describing an animation effect. 

An animation effect can be the combination of a motion and an optional fade effect, e.\+g\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{AnimationEffect::SlideInFromRight}
\DoxyCodeLine{AnimationEffect::SlideInFromTop | AnimationEffect::Fade}
\end{DoxyCode}


You can specify only one motion effect.

\index{Wt@{Wt}!EntryPointType@{EntryPointType}}
\index{EntryPointType@{EntryPointType}!Wt@{Wt}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{EntryPointType}{EntryPointType}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum Wt\+::\+Entry\+Point\+Type\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [strong]}}



Enumeration that indicates a Wt entrypoint type. 

An entry point binds a behavior to a public U\+RL. Only the wthttpd connector currently supports multiple entry points. \begin{DoxyEnumFields}{Enumerator}
\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{Application@{Application}!Wt@{Wt}}\index{Wt@{Wt}!Application@{Application}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{classWt_af4b6ed5fd28b4f5fa141b153c1107349ae498749f3c42246d50b15c81c101d988}\label{classWt_af4b6ed5fd28b4f5fa141b153c1107349ae498749f3c42246d50b15c81c101d988}} 
Application&Specifies a full-\/screen application. A full screen application manages the entire browser window and provides its own H\+T\+ML page.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WServer_af2b8ea616bee5bd63e6294bad3d7574e}{W\+Server\+::add\+Entry\+Point()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WApplication_a485af3ad2b758931edbde77fcf529981}{W\+Application\+::root()}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{WidgetSet@{WidgetSet}!Wt@{Wt}}\index{Wt@{Wt}!WidgetSet@{WidgetSet}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{classWt_af4b6ed5fd28b4f5fa141b153c1107349accf2281a355c2c9cd4698ac30bea7820}\label{classWt_af4b6ed5fd28b4f5fa141b153c1107349accf2281a355c2c9cd4698ac30bea7820}} 
Widget\+Set&Specifies an application that manages one or more widgets. A widget set application is part of an existing H\+T\+ML page. One or more H\+T\+ML elements in that web page may be bound to widgets managed by the application.

The application presents itself as a Java\+Script file, and therefore should be embedded in the web page using a $<$script$>$ tag, from within the $<$body$>$ (since it needs access to the $<$body$>$).

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
A Entry\+Point\+Type\+::\+Widget\+Set application requires Java\+Script support
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WServer_af2b8ea616bee5bd63e6294bad3d7574e}{W\+Server\+::add\+Entry\+Point()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WApplication_abf3104dc9f6d7b491d8ef5194332525d}{W\+Application\+::bind\+Widget()}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\\

Static\+Resource&Specifies a static resource. A static resource binds a \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WResource}{W\+Resource}} to a public U\+RL, and is not bound to a specific session. \\

\mbox{\Hypertarget{classWt_a2551043da5512cfe7b857c5db6e5ae40}\label{classWt_a2551043da5512cfe7b857c5db6e5ae40}} 
\index{Wt@{Wt}!PositionScheme@{PositionScheme}}
\index{PositionScheme@{PositionScheme}!Wt@{Wt}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{PositionScheme}{PositionScheme}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum Wt\+::\+Position\+Scheme\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [strong]}}



Enumeration that specifies a layout mechanism for a widget. 

The layout mechanism determines how the widget positions itself relative to the parent or sibling widgets.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WWidget_ae15ffe92fdc5c394013d61b5bebb2f11}{W\+Widget\+::set\+Position\+Scheme(\+Position\+Scheme scheme)}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\begin{DoxyEnumFields}{Enumerator}
\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{Static@{Static}!Wt@{Wt}}\index{Wt@{Wt}!Static@{Static}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{classWt_a2551043da5512cfe7b857c5db6e5ae40a84a8921b25f505d0d2077aeb5db4bc16}\label{classWt_a2551043da5512cfe7b857c5db6e5ae40a84a8921b25f505d0d2077aeb5db4bc16}} 
Static&Static position scheme. The widget is layed-\/out with other \mbox{\hyperlink{}{Static}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{}{Relative}} sibling widgets, one after another.

Inline widgets are layed out in horizontal lines (like text), wrapping around at the end of the line to continue on the next line. Block widgets are stacked vertically.

Static widgets may also float to the left or right border, using set\+Float\+Side(). \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{Relative@{Relative}!Wt@{Wt}}\index{Wt@{Wt}!Relative@{Relative}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{classWt_a2551043da5512cfe7b857c5db6e5ae40a2ca9469819fb0fb61ff98e914a7ccca0}\label{classWt_a2551043da5512cfe7b857c5db6e5ae40a2ca9469819fb0fb61ff98e914a7ccca0}} 
Relative&Relative position scheme. The widget is first layed out according to Static layout rules, but after layout, the widget may be offset relative to where it would be in a static layout, using set\+Offsets().

Another common use of a Relative position scheme (even with no specified offsets) is to provide a new reference coordinate system for Absolutely positioned widgets. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{Absolute@{Absolute}!Wt@{Wt}}\index{Wt@{Wt}!Absolute@{Absolute}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{classWt_a2551043da5512cfe7b857c5db6e5ae40ab51ca26c6c89cfc9bec338f7a0d3e0c8}\label{classWt_a2551043da5512cfe7b857c5db6e5ae40ab51ca26c6c89cfc9bec338f7a0d3e0c8}} 
Absolute&Absolute position scheme. The widget is positioned at an absolute position with respect to the nearest ancestor widget that is either\+: 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item a \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WTableCell}{W\+Table\+Cell}}  
\item or has a position scheme that is \mbox{\hyperlink{}{Relative}} or \mbox{\hyperlink{}{Absolute}}.  
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{Fixed@{Fixed}!Wt@{Wt}}\index{Wt@{Wt}!Fixed@{Fixed}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{classWt_a2551043da5512cfe7b857c5db6e5ae40a4457d440870ad6d42bab9082d9bf9b61}\label{classWt_a2551043da5512cfe7b857c5db6e5ae40a4457d440870ad6d42bab9082d9bf9b61}} 
Fixed&Fixed position scheme. The widget is positioned at fixed position with respect to the browser\textquotesingle{}s view-\/pane. \\
\hline

\end{DoxyEnumFields}

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{SetId@{SetId}!Wt@{Wt}}\index{Wt@{Wt}!SetId@{SetId}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{classWt_a323dcef5293055d85c57d23ec1936a26aacf51340a8e3d9c543cb3e77d8845636}\label{classWt_a323dcef5293055d85c57d23ec1936a26aacf51340a8e3d9c543cb3e77d8845636}} 
Set\+Id&Use set\+Id() to set the ID as the var\+Name.

\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
You must be careful that there are no two widgets with the same ID in yor application. 
\end{DoxyWarning}
\\
